1A - G   31792 - 32  (01/2020)
 THE  SRI  LANKA  ARMED  SERVICES  LONG  SERVICE  MEDAL
IT is hereby notified that His Excellency the President of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and the Commander
in Chief of the Armed Forces have been pleased to approve the award of the Sri Lanka Armed Services Long Service
Medal to the persons specified in the schedule here.
By His Excellency’s Command,
Major General (Rtd.) K
AMAL GUNARATNE, WWV RWP RSP USP ndc psc,
Secretary,
 Ministry of Defence.
Ministry of Defence,
Colombo.
08th January, 2020.
